***symboliek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:symboliek.html>symboliek</a> (29031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">symbolique</i>. The sense “theological study of symbolism” <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Symbolik</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:symbool.html>symbool</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-iek</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:symboliek.html>symboliek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:symboliek.html>symbolieken</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>symbolism</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the theological study of symbolism</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">symbole</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">symbolum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σύμβολον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">súmbolon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Middle Dutch used the Latin form <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">symbolum</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:synthetiseren.html>synthetiseren</a> (112472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">synthétiser</i> (from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">synthèse</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">synthesis</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span>), cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">synthesize</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">synthetisieren</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:synthetiseren.html>synthetiseren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To synthesize, make a synthesis, summarise</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To (re)produce synthetically, e.g. using substitute ingredients</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">make a synthesis</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:samenvatten.html>samenvatten</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">synthetisering</span>, (obsolete) <span class="Latn" lang="nl">synthetiseering</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:synthese.html>synthese</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:synthetisch.html>synthetisch</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:synthetiseren.html>synthetiseren</a></b>

***taai.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:taai.html>taai</a> (5121)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">taey</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tāi</i>, from earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tāhi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tanhuz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zäh</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tough</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:taai.html>taai</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:taaier.html>taaier</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">taaist</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tough, resilient</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of food</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> difficult to chew</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>taal</a> (1749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tāle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tala</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*talō</i>.

***tabak.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tabak.html>tabak</a> (7615)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">tabaco</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabak.html>tabak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabak.html>tabakken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabak.html>tabakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The tobacco plant.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Tobacco, the product made from leaves of certain of its varieties, to be smoked in cigars etc., sniffed or chewed.</li></ol>

***tabel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tabel.html>tabel</a> (42983)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Tabelle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tabella</i>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabula.html>tabula</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tablet, board, <a href = vnd.unilang:plank.html>plank</a>, chart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Originally the older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafel.html>tafel</a></i> (which derives ultimately from the same Latin source and thus <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> its doublet) <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> used alongside <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabel.html>tabel</a></i> with the same meaning, still seen in the use of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafel.html>tafel</a></i> to mean a multiplication table. <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>Over</a> time, it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> differentiated from it.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabel.html>tabel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabellen.html>tabellen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabel.html>tabelletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>table (grid of data in rows and <a href = vnd.unilang:columns.html>columns</a>)</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">voedingswaardetabel</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">tabulair</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tabel.html>tabel</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> geordende <a href = vnd.unilang:lijst.html>lijst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gegevens.html>gegevens</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:overzichtelijk.html>overzichtelijker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> in <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tabellen.html>tabellen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zet.html>zet</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabernakel.html>tabernakel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tabernaculum</i>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">taberna</i>.
</p>

***tabula.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tabula.html>tabula</a> (53098)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The origin <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> uncertain. Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*th₂-dʰlom</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*teh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (a variety of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*steh₂-</i> without s-mobile, whence also Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">stō, stāre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*-dʰlom</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">instrumental suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> whence Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-bula</i>. The original meaning would then be “that which stands”, for which see also Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">stabulum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabula.html>tabula</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">tabulae</b>); <i>first declension</i>
</p>
<ol><li>tablet, sometimes a tablet covered with wax for writing</li>
<li>board or <a href = vnd.unilang:plank.html>plank</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> map, painting, document or other item put onto a tablet</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">map</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="la">charta</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="la">fōrma</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="la">tabella</span></li>

***tafel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tafel.html>tafel</a> (916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tâfele</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tavala</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabula.html>tabula</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">board</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tabel.html>tabel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafel.html>tafel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafels.html>tafels</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafelen.html>tafelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafeltje.html>tafeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>table (item of furniture)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">dis</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> meal, spread on (a) table(s)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maaltijd.html>maaltijd</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maal.html>maal</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">arithmetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> multiplication table</li>
<li>writing tablet
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">tablet</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The plural <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafelen.html>tafelen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> only used in the sense "writing tablet".

***tailback.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tailback.html>tailback</a> (59042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tail</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">back</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tailback.html>tailback</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tailbacks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A line of <a href = vnd.unilang:motor.html>motor</a> vehicles causing or the result of traffic congestion or a traffic jam; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> backup.
<ul><li><b>2013</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> Jenkins, <i>Gibraltar and the Falklands deny the logic of history</i> (in <i>The Guardian</i>, 14 August 2013)<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2013/aug/14/gibraltar-falklands-deny-logic-history">[1]</a>
<dl><dd>The idea of a British warship supposedly menacing Spain <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ludicrous. <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> it meant to bomb Cadiz? Will its <a href = vnd.unilang:guns.html>guns</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lift.html>lift</a> a rush-hour <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tailback.html>tailback</a></b> in a colony that most Britons regard as awash with tax <a href = vnd.unilang:dodgers.html>dodgers</a>, drug <a href = vnd.unilang:dealers.html>dealers</a> and right-wing whingers? The Gibraltarians have rights, but why British taxpayers should send warships to enforce them, <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> if just "on exercise", <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a mystery.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">American football</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A running back or <a href = vnd.unilang:halfback.html>halfback</a> who lines up furthest to the rear in an I formation.</li></ol>
</body>

***takelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:takelen.html>takelen</a> (36600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:takel.html>takel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:takelen.html>takelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hoist with a tackle or pulley</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> nautical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rig <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of sailing vessels</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuigen.html>tuigen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aftakelen.html>aftakelen</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">takelaar</span></li>

***taks.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:taks.html>taks</a> (53091)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">taxe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">taxe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">taxa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:taks.html>taks</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:taksen.html>taksen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:taks.html>taksje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">tax</span></li>
<li>fee, amount, share</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:taks.html>Taks</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a common Belgian Dutch word for “tax”. The equivalent term in the Netherlands <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belasting.html>belasting</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:taks.html>taks</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> more limited use there, mostly for brevity and in fixed expressions like <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vlaktaks</i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belasting.html>belasting</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heffing.html>heffing</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">milieutaks</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">vlaktaks</span></li></ul>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:taks.html>taks</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:zoogdieren.html>zoogdieren</a>)</span> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> dashond <sup id="cite_ref-qtaks2_2-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-qtaks2-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tālen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:talon.html>talon</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*talōną</i>.
